  The Dockerfile has been created with the basic structure for setting up the RelTR environment. It successfully installs system dependencies, clones the repository, and downloads Miniconda. However, the build fails when trying to create a conda environment with Python 3.6, likely due to compatibility issues with the latest Miniconda version that may not support Python 3.6.
  next step

Alternatively, use Anaconda instead of Miniconda, or modify the Python version requirement to a more recent version (e.g., Python 3.7 or 3.8) if the codebase allows it.

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV PATH="/root/miniconda3/bin:${PATH}"
  ENV CONDA_AUTO_UPDATE_CONDA=false
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      wget \
      build-essential \
      unzip \
      curl \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  WORKDIR /workspace
  RUN git clone https://github.com/yrcong/RelTR.git
  WORKDIR /workspace/RelTR
  RUN wget https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh && \
      bash Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -b -p /root/miniconda3 && \
      rm Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh
  RUN /root/miniconda3/bin/conda init bash && \
      echo "conda activate reltr" >> ~/.bashrc
  RUN /root/miniconda3/bin/conda create -n reltr python=3.6 -y
  SHELL ["/root/miniconda3/bin/conda", "run", "-n", "reltr", "/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN conda install pytorch==1.6.0 torchvision==0.7.0 cpuonly -c pytorch -y && \
      conda install matplotlib -y && \
      conda install scipy=1.5.2 -y && \
      pip install -U 'git+https://github.com/cocodataset/cocoapi.git#subdirectory=PythonAPI'
  RUN mkdir -p ckpt data/vg/images data/oi/images
  WORKDIR /workspace/RelTR/lib/fpn
  RUN chmod +x make.sh && \
      ./make.sh || true
  WORKDIR /workspace/RelTR
  RUN find . -type d -name __pycache__ -exec rm -rf {} + || true
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash' > /entrypoint.sh && \
      echo 'source /root/miniconda3/etc/profile.d/conda.sh' >> /entrypoint.sh && \
      echo 'conda activate reltr' >> /entrypoint.sh && \
      echo 'exec "$@"' >> /entrypoint.sh && \
      chmod +x /entrypoint.sh
  ENTRYPOINT ["/entrypoint.sh"]
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV PATH="/root/miniconda3/bin:${PATH}"
  ENV CONDA_AUTO_UPDATE_CONDA=false
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      wget \
      build-essential \
      unzip \
      curl \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  WORKDIR /workspace
  RUN git clone https://github.com/yrcong/RelTR.git
  WORKDIR /workspace/RelTR
  RUN wget https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-py37_4.10.3-Linux-x86_64.sh && \
      bash Miniconda3-py37_4.10.3-Linux-x86_64.sh -b -p /root/miniconda3 && \
      rm Miniconda3-py37_4.10.3-Linux-x86_64.sh
  RUN /root/miniconda3/bin/conda init bash && \
      echo "conda activate reltr" >> ~/.bashrc
  RUN /root/miniconda3/bin/conda create -n reltr python=3.6 -y
  SHELL ["/root/miniconda3/bin/conda", "run", "-n", "reltr", "/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN conda install pytorch==1.6.0 torchvision==0.7.0 cpuonly -c pytorch -y && \
      conda install matplotlib -y && \
      conda install scipy=1.5.2 -y && \
      pip install -U 'git+https://github.com/cocodataset/cocoapi.git#subdirectory=PythonAPI'
  RUN mkdir -p ckpt data/vg/images data/oi/images
  WORKDIR /workspace/RelTR/lib/fpn
  RUN chmod +x make.sh && \
      ./make.sh || true
  WORKDIR /workspace/RelTR
  RUN find . -type d -name __pycache__ -exec rm -rf {} + || true
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash' > /entrypoint.sh && \
      echo 'source /root/miniconda3/etc/profile.d/conda.sh' >> /entrypoint.sh && \
      echo 'conda activate reltr' >> /entrypoint.sh && \
      echo 'exec "$@"' >> /entrypoint.sh && \
      chmod +x /entrypoint.sh
  ENTRYPOINT ["/entrypoint.sh"]
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV PATH="/root/miniconda3/bin:${PATH}"
  ENV CONDA_AUTO_UPDATE_CONDA=false
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      wget \
      build-essential \
      unzip \
      curl \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  WORKDIR /workspace
  RUN git clone https://github.com/yrcong/RelTR.git
  WORKDIR /workspace/RelTR
  RUN wget https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-py37_4.10.3-Linux-x86_64.sh && \
      bash Miniconda3-py37_4.10.3-Linux-x86_64.sh -b -p /root/miniconda3 && \
      rm Miniconda3-py37_4.10.3-Linux-x86_64.sh
  RUN /root/miniconda3/bin/conda init bash && \
      echo "conda activate reltr" >> ~/.bashrc
  RUN /root/miniconda3/bin/conda create -n reltr python=3.6 -y
  SHELL ["/root/miniconda3/bin/conda", "run", "-n", "reltr", "/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN conda install pytorch==1.6.0 torchvision==0.7.0 cpuonly -c pytorch -y && \
      conda install matplotlib -y && \
      conda install scipy=1.5.2 -y && \
      pip install -U 'git+https://github.com/cocodataset/cocoapi.git#subdirectory=PythonAPI'
  RUN mkdir -p ckpt data/vg/images data/oi/images
  WORKDIR /workspace/RelTR/lib/fpn
  RUN chmod +x make.sh && \
      ./make.sh || true
  WORKDIR /workspace/RelTR
  RUN find . -type d -name __pycache__ -exec rm -rf {} + || true
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash' > /workspace/entrypoint.sh && \
      echo 'source /root/miniconda3/etc/profile.d/conda.sh' >> /workspace/entrypoint.sh && \
      echo 'conda activate reltr' >> /workspace/entrypoint.sh && \
      echo 'exec "$@"' >> /workspace/entrypoint.sh && \
      chmod +x /workspace/entrypoint.sh
  ENTRYPOINT ["/workspace/entrypoint.sh"]
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV PATH="/root/miniconda3/bin:${PATH}"
  ENV CONDA_AUTO_UPDATE_CONDA=false
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      wget \
      build-essential \
      unzip \
      curl \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  WORKDIR /workspace
  RUN git clone https://github.com/yrcong/RelTR.git
  RUN wget https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-py37_4.10.3-Linux-x86_64.sh && \
      bash Miniconda3-py37_4.10.3-Linux-x86_64.sh -b -p /root/miniconda3 && \
      rm Miniconda3-py37_4.10.3-Linux-x86_64.sh
  RUN /root/miniconda3/bin/conda init bash && \
      echo "conda activate reltr" >> ~/.bashrc
  RUN /root/miniconda3/bin/conda create -n reltr python=3.6 -y
  SHELL ["/root/miniconda3/bin/conda", "run", "-n", "reltr", "/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN conda install pytorch==1.6.0 torchvision==0.7.0 cpuonly -c pytorch -y && \
      conda install matplotlib -y && \
      conda install scipy=1.5.2 -y && \
      pip install -U 'git+https://github.com/cocodataset/cocoapi.git#subdirectory=PythonAPI'
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash' > /workspace/entrypoint.sh && \
      echo 'source /root/miniconda3/etc/profile.d/conda.sh' >> /workspace/entrypoint.sh && \
      echo 'conda activate reltr' >> /workspace/entrypoint.sh && \
      echo 'exec "$@"' >> /workspace/entrypoint.sh && \
      chmod +x /workspace/entrypoint.sh
  WORKDIR /workspace/RelTR
  RUN mkdir -p ckpt data/vg/images data/oi/images
  WORKDIR /workspace/RelTR/lib/fpn
  RUN chmod +x make.sh && \
      ./make.sh || true
  WORKDIR /workspace/RelTR
  RUN find . -type d -name __pycache__ -exec rm -rf {} + || true
  ENTRYPOINT ["/workspace/entrypoint.sh"]
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV PATH="/root/miniconda3/bin:${PATH}"
  ENV CONDA_AUTO_UPDATE_CONDA=false
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      wget \
      build-essential \
      unzip \
      curl \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  WORKDIR /workspace
  RUN git clone https://github.com/yrcong/RelTR.git
  RUN wget https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-py37_4.10.3-Linux-x86_64.sh && \
      bash Miniconda3-py37_4.10.3-Linux-x86_64.sh -b -p /root/miniconda3 && \
      rm Miniconda3-py37_4.10.3-Linux-x86_64.sh
  RUN /root/miniconda3/bin/conda init bash && \
      echo "conda activate reltr" >> ~/.bashrc
  RUN /root/miniconda3/bin/conda create -n reltr python=3.6 -y
  SHELL ["/root/miniconda3/bin/conda", "run", "-n", "reltr", "/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN conda install pytorch==1.6.0 torchvision==0.7.0 cpuonly -c pytorch -y && \
      conda install matplotlib -y && \
      conda install scipy=1.5.2 -y && \
      pip install -U 'git+https://github.com/cocodataset/cocoapi.git#subdirectory=PythonAPI'
  WORKDIR /workspace/RelTR
  RUN mkdir -p ckpt data/vg/images data/oi/images
  WORKDIR /workspace/RelTR/lib/fpn
  RUN chmod +x make.sh && \
      ./make.sh || true
  WORKDIR /workspace/RelTR
  RUN find . -type d -name __pycache__ -exec rm -rf {} + || true
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash' > /workspace/RelTR/entrypoint.sh && \
      echo 'source /root/miniconda3/etc/profile.d/conda.sh' >> /workspace/RelTR/entrypoint.sh && \
      echo 'conda activate reltr' >> /workspace/RelTR/entrypoint.sh && \
      echo 'exec "$@"' >> /workspace/RelTR/entrypoint.sh && \
      chmod +x /workspace/RelTR/entrypoint.sh
  ENTRYPOINT ["/workspace/RelTR/entrypoint.sh"]
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV PATH="/root/miniconda3/bin:${PATH}"
  ENV CONDA_AUTO_UPDATE_CONDA=false
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      wget \
      build-essential \
      unzip \
      curl \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  WORKDIR /workspace
  RUN git clone https://github.com/yrcong/RelTR.git
  RUN wget https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-py37_4.10.3-Linux-x86_64.sh && \
      bash Miniconda3-py37_4.10.3-Linux-x86_64.sh -b -p /root/miniconda3 && \
      rm Miniconda3-py37_4.10.3-Linux-x86_64.sh
  RUN /root/miniconda3/bin/conda init bash && \
      echo "conda activate reltr" >> ~/.bashrc
  RUN /root/miniconda3/bin/conda create -n reltr python=3.6 -y
  SHELL ["/root/miniconda3/bin/conda", "run", "-n", "reltr", "/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN conda install pytorch==1.6.0 torchvision==0.7.0 cpuonly -c pytorch -y && \
      conda install matplotlib -y && \
      conda install scipy=1.5.2 -y && \
      pip install -U 'git+https://github.com/cocodataset/cocoapi.git#subdirectory=PythonAPI'
  WORKDIR /workspace/RelTR
  RUN mkdir -p ckpt data/vg/images data/oi/images
  WORKDIR /workspace/RelTR/lib/fpn
  RUN chmod +x make.sh && \
      ./make.sh || true
  WORKDIR /workspace/RelTR
  RUN find . -type d -name __pycache__ -exec rm -rf {} + || true
  RUN python -c "import torch; print(torch.__version__)"
